src="http://www.thehindu.com/multimedia/dynamic/02518/THSJMHI-W112_G5_21_2518537e.jpg" class="main-image" alt="A shoe factory on fire near Ambur on Thursday.— Photo: SPECIAL ARRANGEMENT" width="318" height="300" title="A shoe factory on fire near Ambur on Thursday.— Photo: SPECIAL ARRANGEMENT"/><div class="photo-caption"><div class="photo-source"></div>A shoe factory on fire near Ambur on Thursday.— Photo: SPECIAL ARRANGEMENT</div></div><div class="article-body"><p class="body">Fire broke out in a shoe factory near Ambur on Thursday morning. The exact cause and worth of property damaged is yet to be ascertained.</p><p class="body">Plastic along with chemicals were stored on the ground floor, and this is where the fire had reportedly started. The fire spread to the third floor damaging export quality shoes, officials said. However, the exact cause of fire is yet to be ascertained.</p><p class="body">The factory is located about 15 kms away from Ambur near Vadapudupattu, Madhanur.</p><p class="body">The Ambur Fire Station had received a call about the fire at about 6.35 a.m. A fire tender from the station rushed to the spot at about 6.50 a.m., followed by four tenders from Gudiyatham, Vaniyambadi, Odugathur and Tirupattur, according to Hussain Sherriff, Station Fire Officer, Ambur.</p><p class="body">District Fire Officer Murugesan rushed to the spot.</p><p class="body">A total of 40 personnel from the Fire and Rescue Services and three Station Fire Officers were engaged in putting off the fire. The fire was put off around 1.15 p.m.</p><p class="body">Police said that they were yet to receive a complaint from the management of the factory.</p><p class="body">They said only after a complaint can the details of property damaged in the fire will be known.</p><script type="text/javascript">$(function() {$('#articleKeywords a').click( function() { var keyword = $(this).text();if
